!Series_title	"Convergent transcriptomic signatures across brain structures in eating disorders and obsessive compulsive disorder"
!Series_geo_accession	"GSE262138"
!Series_status	"Public on Dec 18 2024"
!Series_submission_date	"Mar 21 2024"
!Series_last_update_date	"Dec 18 2024"
!Series_pubmed_id	"39649579"
!Series_summary	"The objective of this study was to delineate the transcriptomic landscapes of the caudate and dorsolateral prefrontal cortex (DLFPC) in individuals with ED and OCD to identify common and distinct molecular pathways that may underlie these disorders."
!Series_overall_design	"A cross-sectional study was conducted, leveraging postmortem brain samples to perform a transcriptomic analysis of the DLPFC and caudate nucleus from 86 control participants, 57 individuals diagnosed with ED, and 27 with OCD."
!Series_type	"Expression profiling by high throughput sequencing"

This matrix was then normalized through the VOOM method." This matrix was then normalized through the VOOM method."
